class="nova-l-flex__item nova-l-flex__item--grow research-detail-middle-section__item" style="flex-basis:0px;flex-grow:2"><div class="nova-c-card nova-c-card--spacing-m nova-c-card--elevation-1-above"><div class="nova-c-card__header nova-c-card__header--spacing-inherit"><h2 class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-l nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-none nova-e-text--color-grey-700">Abstract and Figures</h2></div><div class="nova-c-card__body nova-c-card__body--spacing-inherit"><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-m nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-none nova-e-text--color-grey-800 research-detail-middle-section__abstract" itemProp="description">With the spread of Covid-19, the world of interaction technology research has completely changed. The pandemic has created a higher demand for technologies that allow us to avoid touching devices. Before the pandemic, the world had a harder time understanding the importance of touchless technology, and even then it was not imagined in this context. The gesture-based technologies and hand interaction that have been adopted in research have thus far not been popular outside of research labs. There are several issues in the design, development, and adoption of such technologies that should be addressed in the near future.</div><div class="js-target-figures" id="figures"><div class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname">Franca Garzotto</span></span></a></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Matteo_Valoriani"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/279403461398531-1443626384283_Q64/Matteo_Valoriani.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Matteo Valoriani"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname">Matteo Valoriani</span></span></a></li></ul></div><div class="nova-v-publication-item__stack-item"><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-m nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-none nova-e-text--color-inherit nova-e-text--clamp-3 nova-v-publication-item__description"><span class="js-target-abstract-5f83d9c8d404f lite-page-hidden">Our understanding of the effectiveness of motion-based touchless games for autistic children is limited, because of the small amount of empirical studies and the limits of our current knowledge on autism. This paper offers two contributions. First, we provide a survey and a discussion of the existing literature. Second, we describe a field study that extends the current body of empirical evidence of the potential benefits of touchless motion-based gaming for autistic children. Our research involved five autistic children and one therapist in the experimentation of a set of Kinect games at a therapeutic center for a period of two and a half months. Using standardized therapeutic tests, observations during game sessions, and video analysis of over 20 hours of children&#x27;s activities, we evaluated the learning benefits in relationship to attentional skills and explored several factors in the emotional and behavioral sphere. Our findings show improvements of the considered learning variables and help us to better understand how autistic children experience motion-based touchless play. Overall, our research sheds a light on the opportunities offered full body touchless games for therapy and education of these special users.</span></div></div></div></div><footer Sousa</span></span></a></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Thomas_Pederson"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-none nova-e-text--color-inherit nova-e-text--clamp-3 nova-v-publication-item__description"><span class="js-target-abstract-5f83d9c8d45ba lite-page-hidden">Sterility restrictions in surgical settings make touch-less interaction an interesting solution for surgeons to Interact directly with digital images. The HCI community has already explored several methods for touch-less interaction including those based on camera- based gesture tracking and voice control. In this paper, we present a system for gesture-based interaction with medical images based on a single wristband sensor and capacitive floor sensors, allowing for hand and foot gesture input. The first limited evaluation of the system showed 3n acceptable level of accuracy for 12 different hand &amp; foot gestures: Also users found that our combined hand and foot based gestures are intuitive for providing input.</span></div></div></div></div><footer class="nova-v-publication-item__footer"><div class="nova-v-publication-item__footer-actions"><div class="nova-o-pack class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-l nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-inherit publication-recommendation-item__title"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare gtm-recommendation-item-link" href="publication/303662293_A_touchless_interface_for_interventional_radiology_procedures">A touchless interface for interventional radiology procedures</a></h3><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-grey-500"><span>October 2015</span></div><ul class="nova-e-list nova-e-list--size-m nova-e-list--type-inline nova-e-list--spacing-auto"><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://c5.rgstatic.net/m/4671872220764/images/template/default/profile/profile_default_m.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Sivaramakrishnan K R"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Sivaramakrishnan_K_R">Sivaramakrishnan K R</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/365884469202945-1464245063237_Q64/Kumar_Raja_Gattamaneni.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Kumar Raja Gattamaneni"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Kumar_Raja_Gattamaneni">Kumar Raja Gattamaneni</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/489887926362113-1493809791508_Q64/Chegu_Kumar.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Chegu Girish Kumar"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Chegu_Kumar">Chegu Girish Kumar</a></span></span></li></ul><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-s nova-e-text--color-grey-500 publication-recommendation-item__abstract">Interventional radiology is a medical sub-specialty of radiology which utilizes minimally-invasive image-guided procedures to diagnose and treat diseases in nearly every organ system. The entire process is pivoted on imaging and the way surgeon or doctor interacts with the images to guide him/her through the entire procedure. The process still remains to be a challenge to interact and manipulate <a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent js-lite-click" data-lite="{&quot;click&quot;:[{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;.js-target-5f83d9c8d4b0e&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;tc(lite-page-hidden)&quot;},{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;self&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;ac(lite-page-hidden)&quot;}]}">... [Show full abstract]</a><span class="lite-page-hidden js-target-5f83d9c8d4b0e"> objects in an image in sterile medical environment where keyboard, mice and touch screen are potential source of infection. This paper aims at investigating a potential solution with a low-cost, touch-free motion-tracking (hand gestures) device for interactions with image visualization environment. The solution involves a device that tracks a person&#x27;s hand gestures and its motion and custom software that translates motion information obtained with the motion-tracking device into commands to review and manipulate images on a workstation. This solution would yield to a Touchless Sterile Interface for effortless image interactions in Interventional Radiology procedures.</span></div><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent publication-recommendation-item__more publication-recommendation-item__more--redesign" href="publication/303662293_A_touchless_interface_for_interventional_radiology_procedures">View full-text</a></div></div></div></div><div class="nova-o-grid__column data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/832756577734657-1575556048465_Q64/Benjamin_Hatscher.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Benjamin Hatscher"/></picture></span><span Wagner</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/scientific-contributions/Luigi-Grimaldi-2133112892">Luigi Grimaldi</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item">[...]</li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/833926734028800-1575835035136_Q64/Christian_Hansen17.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Christian Hansen"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Christian_Hansen17">Christian Hansen</a></span></span></li></ul><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-s nova-e-text--color-grey-500 publication-recommendation-item__abstract">In dieser Arbeit wird eine M\xc3\xb6glichkeit zur Interaktion mit medizinischen Bilddaten w\xc3\xa4hrend einer Operation oh-ne Verwendung der H\xc3\xa4nde vorgestellt. Hierf\xc3\xbcr wird ein taktiler Fu\xc3\x9fboden zur Interaktion genutzt, der keinerlei ortsgebundene Gegebenheiten, wie z.B. Pedale, ben\xc3\xb6tigt. Im Zuge der Arbeit wurde eine grafische Benutzer-oberfl\xc3\xa4che entwickelt, welche die Manipulation von medizinischen 2D-und <a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent js-lite-click" data-lite="{&quot;click&quot;:[{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;.js-target-5f83d9c8d4e9f&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;tc(lite-page-hidden)&quot;},{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;self&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;ac(lite-page-hidden)&quot;}]}">... [Show full abstract]</a><span class="lite-page-hidden js-target-5f83d9c8d4e9f"> 3D-Bilddaten mit Hilfe der F\xc3\xbc\xc3\x9fe erm\xc3\xb6glicht. Die grafische Benutzeroberfl\xc3\xa4che soll das fehlende haptische Feedback des taktilen Fu\xc3\x9fbodens und die flexible r\xc3\xa4umliche wie funktionale Belegung geeignet visualisieren und kommunizieren. Das System wurde im Rahmen einer Nutzerstudie mit 10 Teilnehmern evaluiert. Die Ergebnisse der Studie zeigen die grunds\xc3\xa4tzliche Eignung taktiler Fu\xc3\x9fb\xc3\xb6den als Benutzerschnittstelle, eine steile Lernkurve bei der Nutzung des Systems, aber auch Defizite bei der ausschlie\xc3\x9flichen Verwendung von Taps und Buttons zur Fu\xc3\x9finteraktion.</span></div><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent publication-recommendation-item__more publication-recommendation-item__more--redesign" href="publication/319963265_Navigation_in_medizinischen_Bilddaten_mittels_eines_taktilen_Fussbodens">View full-text</a></div></div></div></div><div class="nova-o-grid__column nova-o-grid__column--width-6/12@m-up publication-recommendation-item__item"><div class="nova-c-card nova-c-card--spacing-m nova-l-flex--wrap-wrap@s-up publication-recommendation-item__item-badges"><div class="nova-l-flex__item"><span class="nova-e-badge nova-e-badge--color-green nova-e-badge--display-inline nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-inherit publication-recommendation-item__title"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare gtm-recommendation-item-link" href="publication/286605736_GPU-Based_Realtime_Hand_Gesture_Interaction_and_Rendering_for_Volume_Datasets_Using_Leap_Motion">GPU-Based Realtime Hand Gesture Interaction and Rendering for Volume Datasets Using Leap Motion</a></h3><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-grey-500"><span>December 2014</span></div><ul class="nova-e-list nova-e-list--size-m nova-e-list--type-inline nova-e-list--spacing-auto"><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span href="https://www.researchgate.net/scientific-contributions/2088306119-Xingce-Wang">Xingce Wang</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item">[...]</li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-s nova-e-text--color-grey-500 publication-recommendation-item__abstract">Touch less interaction has received considerable attention in recent years with benefit of removing the burden of physical contact. To achieve mid-air interaction, several strategies are available. However, since most of these techniques directly map the 2D WIMP GUI to 3D user interface, they lead unnatural result. In this paper, interaction gestures and tools for exploring volume dataset are <a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent js-lite-click" data-lite="{&quot;click&quot;:[{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;.js-target-5f83d9c8d540c&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;tc(lite-page-hidden)&quot;},{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;self&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;ac(lite-page-hidden)&quot;}]}">... [Show full abstract]</a><span class="lite-page-hidden js-target-5f83d9c8d540c"> designed to perform the similar tasks in the real world. We mainly employ the idea of focus + context based on GPU volume ray casting by trapezoid-shaped transfer function when designing interaction tools. User studies are conducted to demonstrate the usability and intuitiveness of our method. The experimental results show a significant advantage in completion time after a short period of training.</span></div><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent publication-recommendation-item__more publication-recommendation-item__more--redesign" nova-c-card__body--spacing-inherit"><div class="publication-recommendation-item publication-recommendation-item--redesign"><div class="nova-l-flex__item nova-l-flex nova-l-flex--gutter-xxs nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-inherit publication-recommendation-item__title"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare gtm-recommendation-item-link" href="publication/336870238_Exploring_the_Use_of_Augmented_Reality_in_a_Kinesthetic_Learning_Application_Integrated_with_an_Intelligent_Virtual_Embodied_Agent">Exploring the Use of Augmented Reality in a Kinesthetic Learning Application Integrated with an Inte...</a></h3><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-xs nova-e-text--color-grey-500"><span>October 2019</span></div><ul class="nova-e-list nova-e-list--size-m nova-e-list--type-inline nova-e-list--spacing-auto"><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/918978947993601-1596113063389_Q64/Muhammad_Iqbal172.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Muhammad Zahid Iqbal"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Muhammad_Iqbal172">Muhammad Zahid Iqbal</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" Campbell</a></span></span></li><li class="nova-e-list__item"><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item"><span class="lite-person-inline-item__image"><picture class="lite-page-avatar lite-page-avatar--size-xs lite-page-avatar--radius-full"> <img src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mN89OjNfwAJDwOxHEacwgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==" data-src="https://i1.rgstatic.net/ii/profile.image/810169629941762-1570170900902_Q64/Eleni_Mangina.jpg" class="lite-image" alt="Eleni Mangina"/></picture></span><span class="nova-v-person-inline-item__fullname"><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-inherit nova-e-link--theme-bare" href="https://www.researchgate.net/profile/Eleni_Mangina">Eleni Mangina</a></span></span></li></ul><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-s nova-e-text--color-grey-500 publication-recommendation-item__abstract">Technology in education is rapidly changing the way that students learn. This allows for the creation of learning tools that provide better interaction, creative engagement and adaptability to a learner. Augmented Reality (AR) is one of these emerging technologies which can facilitate the development of new learning tools. AR has successfully been proven to allow new types of learning pedagogies <a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent js-lite-click" data-lite="{&quot;click&quot;:[{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;.js-target-5f83d9c8d5bc6&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;tc(lite-page-hidden)&quot;},{&quot;t&quot;:&quot;self&quot;,&quot;a&quot;:&quot;ac(lite-page-hidden)&quot;}]}">... [Show full abstract]</a><span class="lite-page-hidden js-target-5f83d9c8d5bc6"> by providing human-centered learning environments. In particular, the pedagogical approach of Kinesthetic learning or &quot;Learning by Doing&quot; has not been explored in great detail in combination with Augmented Reality. This approach is to physically act out an activity to aid in the learning process and has been previously proven as one of the most successful approaches. For a successful application of this pedagogy, the student must get precise feedback and be guided through a process, thus some form of intelligent guide needs to be actively monitoring the learning environment. This paper presents the exploration of this concept through the presentation of an initial prototype system that was developed and implemented based on an adaptive learning methodology within an AR application, with the prospect that in the future will use intelligent agents.</span></div><a class="nova-e-link nova-e-link--color-blue nova-e-link--theme-silent publication-recommendation-item__more publication-recommendation-item__more--redesign" full-text</a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="nova-e-text nova-e-text--size-s nova-e-text--family-sans-serif nova-e-text--spacing-none
